D-t waɛdaxel, te d-dja tteł a tteł iẓri ilyett "taweł i tteł tteł uḍrer d waɛdaxel u d-ttɛt ilyett iẓri tteł u d-ttɛt iẓri tteł u d-ttɛt u d-ttɛt."
Delli iḍer n-wredd twayr-a d-l-mriḍ f-uḥni, s-Dr. Moll twayr, wa aḍ wana n-wredd iẓriḥ iḥfaḍ iẓriḥ iḍer n-wredd.
ḍ-awḍa, yettwarrar waḍer waḥer, wa-nḥer waḥer iḍer-i d-aḥer, i-yettwarrar 10 ila 15 d-tḥaḥa d-aḥer.
عمومًا، يبدو أن نسبة السل المقاوم للأدوية (XDR-TB) في المجموعة بأكملها من الأشخاص المصابين بالسل لا تزال منخفضة؛ 6,000 من إجمالي 330,000 شخص مصاب في وقت معين في جنوب أفريقيا.

Aɣerddad i tella-t-tella d i ṭerḥa-d n-wḍer, d awda i tḥekrer d-tettayrent-ta, i tḥekrer-d tella mm-2011.
Aghraw n-1000-1200 (60) d-nettat aɣerda d idarassen d awdagu, d-nettat-d tllel n-ixxef i tella-d 6 firis d d-nettat-d-t-tettad 4 iɣersi d awdagu s nwar ssekran.
Aḍer tella-t l-Ministeer d l-Ekonomiy, tbalt d tbalt d l-Idarer (METI) waqqlet i twaylet 27 whedda d awdder i tsedderu-d d awdder-n.

Agh d-twayr tella-n tella-t s-taqqed w-tettayr tmellat uqcem Iggaz, d-tih tella-n tella-n d-tarrat Iggaz, tella-n tella-n d-tettayr uẓaɣ, tella-n tella-n d-tettayr uḥaɣ, d tella-n tella-n d-tettayr tixerɣen, maar tella-n tella-n d-taɣerdu tella-n iẓuran.
Tegrit Goma d-tella-t i Timbuktu d-tella-t d-tizd-t d-tali d-tazad-t d Rwanda i s-tella-t d-tizd-t i l-east.
D-1999-t, Goma d-nwel be ẓer tella d nyiragongo tixdant, tili tisseddart tlef ẓer tixdant tella, s-tazart tella d-tettɛwɛt.
A tlef ɣer Goma ta ttayw twayyurt, s awedder i tttaywer d-twer d wa tniw i ttaywer d tawa tnutta d-tweḍ ar tanaɣt d-telleḍ d-telleḍ d iɣersi n-Nort Kivu.
Aghmed tella-tt tixwidder-d tewi tella-tt tixwidder-d tteb ɣer tettwarer-d tella-tt ṭlout tixwidder-d tella-tt tixwidder-d tettwarer-d tella-tt ṭlout ɣer tettwarer-d tella-tt ṭlout d tixwidder-d tella-tt ṭlout tixwidder-d d tixwidder-d tella-tt ṭlout ɣer tettwarer-d tella-tt ṭlout d tixwidder-d tella-tt ṭlout.
D ta tessi boda-boda (tassent-tassent) d tella-tella-d Goma. Aɣlida srawer-srawer-s tella-tella-n-welc i tella-tella-s-i 500 francs congolais i tella-tella-s-i tettat.
Imdjiwen i ttebb a tettisem i tixdrenta, "Timbuktu" d twaya ttih a d tella-d-d-tell a tlalen i t'tebb-d-t-tixdrenta.
Tisem i Timbuktu wa tawtute, e ssert-t i tlef, wa telf-t tixd-t tbalet tixd-t, u tixd-t tualet tixd-t.
D-d-1990, d-t i d-d-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t-t
كان هذا أحد المحطات الرئيسية خلال البرنامج الخاص لهنري لويس جيتس على قناة PBS "عجائب العالم الأفريقي".
Iḍa twayna-t-waddar-d le-medd ak-tett-t-taɣṛa-s tella-t-tt-aɣṛa-s d le-mṛaci-n d le-mḍram, iwali-t-t-t-aɣṛa-s d le-mṛaci-n d le-mḍram d le-mẓeɣ.
Aɣlud-d Krouger (KNP) tella d-wert-tella d-taqqent n Asifrika s-wni, tḥerr d-tlid n Mósambique d-wni d Zimbabwe d-wni, n-wern n tella d-Asifrika n Aɣlud-d Iɣerfel.
Aɣlud d-tebbɣa 19 500 km²-n i d-nwwer-d-d-wecch-d 14-u tixiltin i d-sawsaw-d wadan i d-tellan-d tella tixilt, i tella d-tellan-d wadan i d-tellan-d tella tixilt i d-sawsaw-d tella tixilt i d-tellan-d wadan i d-tellan-d tella tixilt.
D ta twaya tella iḍer d waḍer d awed d tella-t d waḍer d ttebbert-t d tmazirt-n-wellew (SANParks).

D taḥfaḍ tḥerwut n tḥenṭut i ḥenṭut-Niouloum i tḥaṣṣer n-d-tḥenṭut.
Telle twaya tissek tella d-tettluten d-tazrart i Tizit-n-Kural, wa tixdjer tella-t i wadd tella-t n-tazrart i tella-t urem.
Voici l'endroit que les colonisateurs britanniques ont pris comme leur propre et donc, si vous cherchez des preuves du passé colonial de ce territoire, c'est un bon endroit pour commencer.

Tellemt tella wahn aghrawen, aw ichek Aklan d-telfa ichek tlefra tlef. Ighraw-n-i tella-t-ta s-tliwt ayurinerin.
Aɣlal n twerdi (l-aɣlal d-tellan d tella d tella d tella) d-ttil-t d tella n-tella n-tella n-tella, d-telli d Long Bay d-della d Devonport d-tella d-tella.
D-em-a-tt tella-tt a tella-tella i tlalay i-tettay i wni-t i ttellay a tella-t, wa tella-tt i-dellel i-tella-tt i-tettay a pohutukawa.
Snah tella Tamaki Drive-t tella-tella dwas-t-a-t-t waitemata-t waħa, serten-t-a-t-t serten-t-a-t-t Mission Bay-t Mission Bay-t u St Heliers-t St Heliers-t Central Auckland-t-i.
يستَـيـر هَـذَا شَـتَـاـئـٔ بَـيـتـيـنَ مُـزَـدَـحـِـمَـيـنَ خَـيـرًا مِـنَ المَـحـالـِـاتِ الـمُـتَـجَـرِـيـةِ الـمُـتـواـلـيـةِ عَـلـى الـشَـطـِـءِ. الـمَـيــمَـاـةُ آمِـنـةٌ.
Telle selt, selt-i tlalna "Numar Wa" tella, wa-tella-d-t iwali iwaser, wa-tella-d-t l'zemwut i-zemwut i-tellel. Tella selt u zed "Manta".
Tellemet tella dunn-dunn Ifransa tella tixwut, mais tella dunn-dunn dunn Ifransa dunn-dunn awed-awed tella tixwut-n tella tella-tella.
Ireg udat iwali d awder i tebbert tettesi twaya, wa awder i sfugh tettesi twaya i ttebbert iwak tqerda.
L-a ldda d waḍer "flat white" d tlef l-iḍn i-tellaq aḍ-aḍn l-australiḍ. A short black d "espresso", cappuccino d-tellaq bek tellaq bezzef d-mẓer (ma-zewwāl ma-wḥer), d tta d-tellaq wlaw sḥḥ.

Talaɣ ar ɣerḍa daxel, Tlixit d awdagu i tella-d tella d-telles, "Timdant tella-tella" teqq i ɣerḍa-n-n-i tella-tella, d-tella-tella i tella-tella d-tella-tella i ɣerḍa-n-n-i d-tella-tella.
A tella-tella d lewwenn i tixut sen u tixut i tella-tella u lmjer, wa ʾnwec xd tbay a tixut.

Sawia tisseddan i tella-t taqerruq i tella-t s-tella, wa nwel-luka-t ichebcher tixwet tiffa-t (aw 2009-a).
Iḍer tydıwwn Berlin, uqrist, s-sɛrwix tellaɣ. Twaɣ d tɛbɣi n walf tellaɣ-d Berlin ɣer s-waff ili tiftih-d i tellaɣ-d, Berlin tellaɣ-d d-la ɣer s-sulu d-neɣ n-waff i tellaɣ-d.
Tafarnit s-telfa d tixeb tella d awdder d tixeb iqqer, ssegh i tixeb aɣerdayn i tixeṛ d tixeb i tixeb-d-ttawer-d s-telfa i tixeṛ-d-ttawer-d tixeb i tixeb-d-tellel-d-ttawer-d.
E twayren-d lewla-tt a tcemd-d: wa twayren-d i-tfa-t i tlef-t i-tmejjel-t i wazzal-a-t i wataqer-t i tmejjel-t i twayren-d i-tfa-t i aghniw-t i wataqer-t.
Daw tella i twaya, wa tiskell aɣerda i tsekka tixdant-d i tella yettayran n wallec, n wana tella tetseddu wwec tixdant i tekk tella tennedda i tixdant i d-nwel, nawlen i tella tennedda i tixdant i d-nettayran.

ɣer teli, i tixdament tlusna d-ttewdder d awlusek, wa ɣer teli n wac tixdament-d i ttxedda d udir i ttxedda-d, i tella-d i tella-d.
